## Identifier-layer correction and supersession

It is preserved only as a superseded receipt with zero final adoption: `.superpowers/sdd/task5_fix3/semantic_application_receipt_pre_identity_preservation.json` / `bcd73eb93693d837d954b6a9d97d6716e3fde64ad3f9474f03a92557185b051f`. The complete selection was recomputed after identifier preservation and audited again with 34 fresh sessions.
